<Construct>Solve the following system of equations</Construct>  
<Subject>Algebra</Subject>  
<Question>  
x + 2y = 5  
3x - y = 1  
</Question>  
<Incorrect Answer>x + 2y = 5  
3x - y = 1  
Adding 2y to the second equation to make the y coefficients the same:  
3x - y + 2y = 1 + 2y  
3x + y = 1 + 2y  
x + 2y = 5  
3x + y = 1 + 2y  
Adding the two equations together:  
4x + 3y = 6 + 2y  
4x + y = 6  
</Incorrect Answer>  
<Misconception>When solving simultaneous equations, thinks they can add variables to one of the equations to make terms across the 2 equations identical</Misconception> 



<Construct>Simplify the following expression</Construct>  
<Subject>Algebra</Subject>  
<Question>

</Question>  
<Incorrect Answer>√16</Incorrect Answer>  
<Misconception>Multiplies surds when asked to add</Misconception>

<Misconception>When using the capture-recapture method for sampling, believes you subtract the number marked second from the number caught second to find the best estimate of population size</Misconception>

<Construct>A histogram</Construct>  
<Subject>The number of hours students spend studying per week</Subject>  
<Question>  
Draw a histogram to represent the following data:
 
 Hours | Frequency
-------|----------
 0-5   | 10
 6-10  | 15
 11-15 | 8
 16-20 | 2
</Question>  
<Incorrect Answer>A histogram with the horizontal axis labeled "Cumulative Frequency" and the vertical axis labeled "Hours". The bars are plotted at heights corresponding to the cumulative frequency of each interval. For example, the bar for the 0-5 interval would be 10 units high, the bar for the 6-10 interval would be 25 units high, and so on.</Incorrect Answer>
